2292             else if (tx_r_valid & tx_r_sop)
                      -3-

                    ==>
2296             else
2297                // hold value from one frame to the next.
2298                tx_no_crc_sop <= tx_no_crc_sop;
                    ==>

                 -1-

2306                tx_no_crc_held <= 1'b0;
                    ==>
2307             else if (~en_transmit_sync | collision_int | late_coll_occured |
                      -2-  
2308                      too_many_retries | fifo_underrun | stat_underflow_pend)
2309                // synchronous reset (from software).
2310                tx_no_crc_held <= 1'b0;
                    ==>
2311             else if (start_frame)
                      -3-

2313                // as new frame is read from fifo interface prior to decision

2317                tx_no_crc_held <= tx_no_crc_sop;

2318             else

2331             if (~n_txreset)
                 -1-  
2332                // asynchronous reset.
2333                begin
2334                  no_of_stored_bytes <= 5'h00;
                      ==>
2335                end
2336             else if (~en_transmit_sync | collision_int | late_coll_occured |
                      -2-  
2337                      too_many_retries | fifo_underrun | stat_underflow_pend)

2339                begin
2340                  no_of_stored_bytes <= 5'h00;
                      ==>
2341                end
2342             else if (pfc_or_pause_frame_transmitting)
                      -3-  
2343                // store not used for tx of pause frames.
2344                begin
2345                  no_of_stored_bytes <= no_of_stored_bytes;
                      ==>
2346                end
2347             else if (start_frame)
                      -4-  
2348                // load new value at start of frame.
2349                begin
2350                  no_of_stored_bytes <= new_frame_bytes;
                      ==>
2351                end

                      -5-

2354                // new data being loaded until next start_of_frame, so just shift.
2355                begin
2356                  no_of_stored_bytes <= no_of_stored_bytes - 5'h01;
                      ==>
2357                end
2358             else if (tx_r_valid & ~last_read & ~nibble_sel & (data_type == TYPE_DATA))
                      -6-

2360                // new data being loaded, so shift & load.
2361                begin
2362                  no_of_stored_bytes <= no_of_str_bytes_nxt[4:0] - 5'h01;
                      ==>
2363                end
2364             else if (tx_r_valid & ~last_read & ((nibble_sel & (data_type == TYPE_DATA)) | (data_type == TYPE_PREAMBLE) | (data_type == TYPE_HOLD)))

2365                // no byte shift, but load active from tx fifo, and last_read is not
2366                // blocking new data being loaded, so just load (10/100 mode only)
2367                // also accommodate extra reads during pre-amble when doing single step update of the correction field
2368                begin
2369                  no_of_stored_bytes <= no_of_str_bytes_nxt[4:0];
                      ==>
2370                end
2371             else if (~tx_r_valid & ~nibble_sel & (data_type == TYPE_DATA) & (no_of_stored_bytes != 5'h00))
                      -8-  
2372                // byte shift active, but no load from tx fifo, so just shift.
2373                begin
2374                  no_of_stored_bytes    <= no_of_stored_bytes - 5'h01;
                      ==>
2375                end
2376             else

2378                begin
2379                  no_of_stored_bytes    <= no_of_stored_bytes;
                      ==>

2454             if (~en_transmit_sync)
                 -1-  
2455                // synchronous reset for buffer state machine.
2456                buffer_state_next = R_BUF_INIT;
                    ==>
2457             else if (coll_occured | stat_underflow_pend)
                      -2-  
2458                // state where the buffer control logic waits for the tx fifo to flush.
2459                buffer_state_next = R_BUF_RST1;
                    ==>
2460             else
2461                // decodes for next state of buffer state machine.
2462                case (buffer_state)
                    -3-  
2463       
2464                   R_RD_PEND_INIT:
2465                      // state used to wait for valid response from fifo
2466                      // interface, indicating word is available.
2467                      begin
2468                         if (tx_r_underflow)
                             -4-  
2469                            // underflow condition occurs which shouldn't
2470                            // happen in a properly configured system. SOP has not
2471                            // yet been read so goto flush state. This is impossible
2472                            // when using the DMA.
2473                            buffer_state_next = R_BUF_RST1;
                                ==>
2474                         else if (tx_r_valid & tx_r_err)
                                  -5-  
2475                            begin
2476                               // errored read, return to initialisation state.
2477                               buffer_state_next = R_IDLE1;
                                   ==>
2478                            end
2479                         else if (tx_r_valid & tx_r_sop & tx_r_eop)
                                  -6-  
2480                            begin
2481                               // first word in frame with sop and eop.
2482                               tx_frame_ready = 1'b1;
                                   ==>
2483                               buffer_state_next = R_FRAME_RDY_EOP;
2484                            end
2485                         else if (tx_r_valid & tx_r_sop & ~tx_r_eop)
                                  -7-  
2486                            begin
2487                               // first word in frame with sop.
2488                               tx_frame_ready = 1'b1;
                                   ==>
2489                               buffer_state_next = R_FRAME_RDY;
2490                            end
2491                         else if (tx_r_valid & ~tx_r_sop)
                                  -8-  
2492                            // no sop, so keep reading the fifo.
2493                            buffer_state_next = R_BUF_INIT;
                                ==>
2494                         else
2495                            // wait for tx_r_valid response.
2496                            buffer_state_next = R_RD_PEND_INIT;
                                ==>
2497                      end
2498       
2499                   R_FRAME_RDY_EOP:
2500                      // state used to wait for start_frame from
2501                      // main tx state machine (fifo transfer with
2502                      // sop and eop in same word).
2503                      begin
2504                         tx_frame_ready = 1'b1;
2505                         if (start_frame & ~pfc_or_pause_frame_transmitting)
                             -9-  
2506                            // start frame detected, and only one
2507                            // word transfered from fifo interface.
2508                            buffer_state_next = R_BUF_INIT;
                                ==>
2509                         else
2510                            // wait in current state for start frame.
2511                            buffer_state_next = R_FRAME_RDY_EOP;
                                ==>
2512                      end
2513       
2514                   R_FRAME_RDY:
2515                      // state used to wait for start frame from main tx
2516                      // state machine.
2517                      begin
2518                         tx_frame_ready = 1'b1;
2519                         if (start_frame & ~pfc_or_pause_frame_transmitting)
                             -10-  
2520                            // start frame detected, perform reads.
2521                            buffer_state_next = R_READ;
                                ==>
2522                         else
2523                            buffer_state_next = R_FRAME_RDY;
                                ==>
2524                      end
2525       
2526                   R_READ:
2527                      // state whilst frame in progress, read the transmit fifo whilst 4 or fewer bytes available
2528                      // or 11 if PTP sync correction field needs modification.
2529                      // also do extra reads during pre-amble when 32 bit data and single step update of the correction field
2530                      begin
2531                         if (((no_of_stored_bytes <= 5'b00100) | ((no_of_stored_bytes <= 5'b01011) & oss_correction_field_sync))
                             -11-  
2532                                               & ((data_type == TYPE_DATA) | ((data_type == TYPE_PREAMBLE) & oss_correction_field_sync)))
2533                            begin
2534                               tx_r_rd_int = 1'b1;
                                   ==>
2535                               buffer_state_next = R_RD_PEND;
2536                            end
2537                         else
2538                            // wait for less than 4 bytes available in
2539                            // the input buffer.
2540                            buffer_state_next = R_READ;
                                ==>
2541                      end
2542       
2543                   R_RD_PEND:
2544                      // state waiting for r_valid response from fifo
2545                      // interface.
2546                      begin
2547                         if (tx_r_underflow)
                             -12-  
2548                            begin
2549                               underflow = 1'b1;
                                   ==>
2550                               buffer_state_next = R_BUF_RST1;
2551                            end
2552                         else if (tx_r_valid & tx_r_err)
                                  -13-  
2553                            begin
2554                               underflow = 1'b1;
                                   ==>
2555                               err_underflow = 1'b1;
2556                               buffer_state_next = R_IDLE1;
2557                            end
2558                         else if (tx_r_valid & tx_r_eop)
                                  -14-  
2559                            // last byte of frame being read.
2560                            buffer_state_next = R_BUF_INIT;
                                ==>
2561                         // if you get two SOP's with no intervening EOP then force
2562                         // under-run to error the frame and stop the state machine
2563                         // locking up
2564                         else if (tx_r_valid & tx_r_sop)
                                  -15-  
2565                            begin
2566                               underflow = 1'b1;
                                   ==>
2567                               err_underflow = 1'b1;
2568                               buffer_state_next = R_IDLE1;
2569                            end
2570                         else if (tx_r_valid & ~tx_r_eop)
                                  -16-  
2571                            // more bytes to read as not tx_r_eop.
2572                            buffer_state_next = R_READ;
                                ==>
2573                         else
2574                            // wait for tx_r_valid.
2575                            buffer_state_next = R_RD_PEND;
                                ==>
2576                      end
2577       
2578                   R_IDLE1:
2579                      // state at end frame.
2580                      begin
2581                         buffer_state_next = R_IDLE2;
                             ==>
2582                      end
2583       
2584                   R_IDLE2:
2585                      // state at end frame.
2586                      begin
2587                         buffer_state_next = R_BUF_INIT;
                             ==>
2588                      end
2589       
2590                   R_BUF_RST1:
2591                      // state used to wait for fifo flush to start.
2592                      begin
2593                         if (tx_r_flush_held & ~fifo_underrun)
                             -17-                        
2594                            // hold until fifo is cleared.
2595                            buffer_state_next = R_BUF_RST2;
                                ==>
2596                         else
2597                            // wait in current state.
2598                            buffer_state_next = R_BUF_RST1;
                                ==>
2599                      end
2600       
2601                   R_BUF_RST2:
2602                      // state used to wait while fifo flush takes place.
2603                      begin
2604                         if (~tx_r_flush_held)
                             -18-  
2605                            // wait for tx_r_flushed to go inactive.
2606                            buffer_state_next = R_BUF_INIT;
                                ==>
2607                         else
2608                            // wait in current state.
2609                            buffer_state_next = R_BUF_RST2;
                                ==>
2610                      end
2611       
2612                   default: // R_BUF_INIT:
2613                      // state from reset, wait for frame on fifo interface, indicated
2614                      // by tx_r_data_rdy going high.
2615                      begin
2616                         if (tx_r_data_rdy & ~tx_byte_mode &
                             -19-  
2617                                                  (no_of_stored_bytes <= 5'h04))
2618                            // wait for tx_r_data_rdy and input buffer
2619                            // has less than four bytes stored.
2620                            begin
2621                               buffer_state_next = R_RD_PEND_INIT;
                                   ==>
2622                               tx_r_rd_int = 1'b1;
2623                            end
2624                         else if (tx_r_data_rdy & tx_byte_mode &
                                  -20-  
2625                                  (no_of_stored_bytes <= 5'h05))
2626                            // wait for tx_r_data_rdy and input buffer
2627                            // has less than five bytes stored.
2628                            begin
2629                               buffer_state_next = R_RD_PEND_INIT;
                                   ==>
2630                               tx_r_rd_int = 1'b1;
2631                            end
2632                         else
2633                            // hold in current state.
2634                            buffer_state_next = R_BUF_INIT;
                                ==>

2923                   // 31 bytes could be buffered. 31 bytes = 248 bits, but is stored in a 256bit vector called
2924                   // stored_bit_locn. Since 128bits are loaded,
2925                   // we need transmit_data_buf_new to be 384 bits wide ..
2926                   // Note that since the databuffer itself is p_tx_buf_width
2927                   // bits wide, which is 160 or 216 if TSU is defined, then we need to drop
2928                   // the upper bits of transmit_data_buf_new
2929                   transmit_data_buf_new = {{(384-p_tx_buf_width){1'b0}},transmit_data_buf};
                       ==>

4046                   int_end_frame_cnt[1:0]  <= 2'b00;

4053                end

4488                   tx_deferred_tx_frame   <= 1'b0;
4489                   tx_late_coll_frame     <= 1'b0;
4490                   tx_crs_error_frame     <= 1'b0;
4491                   tx_too_many_retries    <= 1'b0;
4492                   tx_underflow_frame     <= 1'b1;
4493                end
4494             else if (~tx_status_edge & tx_end_frame)
                      -10-  
4495                // hold statistics outputs until taken by
4496                // registers block.
4497                begin
4498                   tx_end_frame           <= 1'b1;
                       ==>
4499                   tx_end_tog             <= tx_end_tog;
4500                   stat_underflow_ack     <= stat_underflow_ack;
4501                   tx_pause_frame_txed    <= tx_pause_frame_txed;
4502                   tx_pfc_pause_frame_txed<= tx_pfc_pause_frame_txed;
4503                   tx_broadcast_frame     <= tx_broadcast_frame;
4504                   tx_multicast_frame     <= tx_multicast_frame;
4505                   tx_frame_txed_ok       <= tx_frame_txed_ok;
4506                   tx_single_coll_frame   <= tx_single_coll_frame;
4507                   tx_multi_coll_frame    <= tx_multi_coll_frame;
4508                   tx_deferred_tx_frame   <= tx_deferred_tx_frame;
4509                   tx_late_coll_frame     <= tx_late_coll_frame;
4510                   tx_crs_error_frame     <= tx_crs_error_frame;
4511                   tx_too_many_retries    <= tx_too_many_retries;
4512                   tx_underflow_frame     <= tx_underflow_frame;
4513                end
4514             else
4515                // clear statistics outputs once taken by
4516                // registers block.
4517                begin
4518                   tx_end_frame           <= 1'b0;
                       ==>

4541             if (~n_txreset)
                 -1-  
4542                // asynchronous reset.
4543                tx_coll_occured <= 1'b0;
                    ==>
4544             else if (~en_transmit_sync)
                      -2-  
4545                // synchronous reset (from software).
4546                tx_coll_occured <= 1'b0;
                    ==>
4547             else if (collision_int & ~dma_eof_noack & ~pclksync_eof_noack)
                      -3-  
4548                // collision occurred and status/statistics update from
4549                // previous frame complete.
4550                tx_coll_occured <= 1'b1;
                    ==>
4551             else if (tx_status_edge)
                      -4-  
4552                // clear status once it has been taken by registers block.
4553                tx_coll_occured <= 1'b0;
                    ==>
4554             else
4555                // else hold value.
4556                tx_coll_occured <= tx_coll_occured;
                    ==>

Branches:
-1--2--3--4-Status
1 - - - Covered
0 1 - - Covered
0 0 1 - Not Covered
0 0 0 1 Covered
0 0 0 0 Covered 



4565             if (~n_txreset)
                 -1-  
4566                begin
4567                   sof_tx <= 1'b0;
                       ==>
4568                end
4569             else if (~tx_en | ~en_transmit_sync)
                      -2-

4571                   sof_tx <= 1'b0;
                       ==>
4572                end

                      -3-

                       ==>
4576                end
                    MISSING_ELSE
                    ==>

4646             case (tx_dec_state)
                 -1-  
4647       
4648                TX_DEC_START : // decode PTP Multicast MAC addresses or IPv4/IPV6 Ethertype
4649                   begin
4650                      // Multicast MAC addresses part1
4651                      if (tx_ptp_count == 7'b0000000)
                          -2-  
4652                         begin
4653                            // address part1 01
4654                            if (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == 8'h01 & (data_type == TYPE_DATA))
                                -3-  
4655                               begin
4656                                  tx_dec_state_nxt = TX_DEC_PTP_1;
                                      ==>
4657                               end
4658                            else
4659                               begin
4660                                  tx_dec_state_nxt = TX_DEC_START;
                                      ==>
4661                               end
4662                         end
4663                      // Ethertype needs IPv4, IPv6 or VLAN type ID
4664                      else if (tx_ptp_count == 7'b0001100)
                               -4-  
4665                         begin
4666                            // IPv6
4667                            if (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == 8'h86)
                                -5-  
4668                               begin
4669                                  tx_dec_state_nxt = TX_DEC_IPV6_1;
                                      ==>
4670                               end
4671                            // IPv4
4672                            else if (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == 8'h08)
                                     -6-  
4673                               begin
4674                                  tx_dec_state_nxt = TX_DEC_IPV4_1;
                                      ==>
4675                               end

                                     -7-

                                      ==>
4680                               end

5063                            else
5064                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
                                   ==>
5065                          end
5066       
5067                      7'b0010001 : // Ethertype2 PTP
5068                         begin
5069                            if (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == 8'hf7)
                                -45-  
5070                              tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_VPTP_2;
                                  ==>
5071                            // invalid - wait for next frame
5072                            else
5073                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
                                   ==>
5074                          end
5075       
5076                      7'b0010010 : // messageType
5077                         begin  // Sync frame for 802.1AS is not supported with VLAN tag
5078                                // so sync frame decode has been removed from this state
5079                            // pdelay_req frame
5080                            if (transmit_data_buf[3:0] == 4'h2)
                                -46-  
5081                               begin
5082                                  tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_VPTP_2;
                                      ==>
5083                                  pdelay_req_tx_nxt = 1'b1;
5084                               end
5085                            // pdelay_resp
5086                            else if (transmit_data_buf[3:0] == 4'h3)
                                     -47-  
5087                               begin
5088                                  tx_dec_state_nxt   = TX_DEC_VPTP_2;
                                      ==>
5089                                  pdelay_resp_tx_nxt = 1'b1;
5090                               end
5091                            // detect General 1588 Messages then wait for next frame and also if
5092                            // invalid - wait for next frame
5093                            else
5094                            begin
5095                              general_frame_tx_nxt =  (transmit_data_buf[3:0] == 4'ha);   // Pdelay_Resp_Follow_Up
                                  ==>
5096                              tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
5097                            end
5098                         end
5099       
5100                      7'b0110100 : // timestamp start position is 34B after messageType
5101                         begin
5102                            tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_VPTP_2;
                                ==>
5103                         end
5104       
5105                      7'b0111101 : // timestamp end position is 9B after timestamp start
5106                         begin
5107                            // this will stop tx_ptp_count after TS finished
5108                            tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
                                ==>
5109                         end
5110       
5111                      default :
5112                         begin
5113                            tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_VPTP_2;
                                ==>
5114                         end
5115       
5116                      endcase
5117                   end
5118       
5119                TX_DEC_IPV4_1 : // decode IPv4
5120                   begin
5121                      case (tx_ptp_count)
                          -48-  
5122                      7'b0001101 : // Ethertype IPv4
5123                         begin
5124                            if (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == 8'h00)
                                -49-  
5125                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV4_1;
                                   ==>
5126                            // invalid - wait for next frame
5127                            else
5128                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
                                   ==>
5129                          end
5130       
5131                      7'b0010111 : // UDP protocol
5132                         begin
5133                            if (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == 8'h11)
                                -50-  
5134                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV4_1;
                                   ==>
5135                            // invalid - wait for next frame
5136                            else
5137                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
                                   ==>
5138                          end
5139       
5140                      7'b0011110 : // IP multicast address 1
5141                         begin
5142                            // PTP primary and peer
5143                            if (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == 8'he0)
                                -51-  
5144                               begin
5145                                  tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV4_1;
5146                                  if (ptp_unicast_ena_sync &
                                      -52-  
5147                                      (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == tx_ptp_unicast[31:24]))
5148                                     ptp_unicast_nxt   = 1'b1;
                                         ==>
                                         MISSING_ELSE
                                         ==>
5149                               end
5150                            // PTP unicast
5151                            else if (ptp_unicast_ena_sync &
                                     -53-  
5152                                     (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == tx_ptp_unicast[31:24]))
5153                               begin
5154                                  tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV4_1;
                                      ==>
5155                                  ptp_unicast_nxt   = 1'b1;
5156                               end
5157                            // invalid - wait for next frame
5158                            else
5159                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
                                   ==>
5160                         end
5161       
5162                      7'b0011111 : // IP multicast address 2
5163                         begin
5164                            // PTP primary and peer, not unicast
5165                            if (~ptp_unicast & (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == 8'h00))
                                -54-  
5166                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV4_1;
                                   ==>
5167                            // PTP unicast
5168                            else if (ptp_unicast &
                                     -55-  
5169                                     (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == tx_ptp_unicast[23:16]))
5170                               begin
5171                                  tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV4_1;
                                      ==>
5172                                  ptp_unicast_nxt   = 1'b1;
5173                               end
5174                            // invalid - wait for next frame
5175                            else
5176                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
                                   ==>
5177                         end
5178       
5179                      7'b0100000 : // IP multicast address 3
5180                         begin
5181                            // PTP primary, not unicast
5182                            if (~ptp_unicast & (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == 8'h01))
                                -56-  
5183                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV4_2;
                                   ==>
5184                            // peer delay, not unicast
5185                            else if (~ptp_unicast & (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == 8'h00))
                                     -57-  
5186                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV4_3;
                                   ==>
5187                            // PTP unicast
5188                            else if (ptp_unicast &
                                     -58-  
5189                                     (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == tx_ptp_unicast[15:8]))
5190                               begin
5191                                  tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV4_2;
                                      ==>
5192                                  ptp_unicast_nxt   = 1'b1;
5193                               end
5194                            // invalid - wait for next frame
5195                            else
5196                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
                                   ==>
5197                         end
5198       
5199                      default :
5200                         begin
5201                            tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV4_1;
                                ==>
5202                         end
5203       
5204                      endcase
5205                   end
5206       
5207                TX_DEC_IPV4_2 : // decode IPv4 PTP primary version 1 and 2
5208                   begin
5209                      case (tx_ptp_count)
                          -59-  
5210       
5211                      7'b0100001 : // IP multicast address 4
5212                         begin
5213                            // PTP primary version 1 and 2 possible, not unicast
5214                            if (~ptp_unicast & (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == 8'h81))
                                -60-  
5215                               begin
5216                                  tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV4_2;
                                      ==>
5217                                  ptp_ver_1_nxt     = 1'b1;
5218                                  ptp_ver_2_nxt     = 1'b1;
5219                               end
5220                            // PTP primary version 1, not unicast
5221                            else if (ptp_primary_nunicast)
                                     -61-  
5222                               begin
5223                                  tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV4_2;
                                      ==>
5224                                  ptp_ver_1_nxt     = 1'b1;
5225                               end
5226                            // PTP unicast
5227                            else if (ptp_unicast &
                                     -62-  
5228                                     (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == tx_ptp_unicast[7:0]))
5229                               begin
5230                                  tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV4_2;
                                      ==>
5231                                  ptp_unicast_nxt   = 1'b1;
5232                                  ptp_ver_2_nxt     = 1'b1;
5233                               end
5234                            // invalid - wait for next frame
5235                            else
5236                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
                                   ==>
5237                         end
5238       
5239                      7'b0100100 : // UDP destination port 1
5240                         begin
5241                            if (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == 8'h01)
                                -63-  
5242                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV4_2;
                                   ==>
5243                            // invalid - wait for next frame
5244                            else
5245                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
                                   ==>
5246                          end
5247       
5248                      7'b0100101 : // UDP destination port 2
5249                         begin
5250                            if (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == 8'h3f)
                                -64-  
5251                               begin
5252                                  tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV4_2;
                                      ==>
5253                                  general_frame_tx_nxt = 1'b0;
5254                               end
5255                            else if (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == 8'h40)
                                     -65-  
5256                               begin
5257                                  tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV4_2;
                                      ==>
5258                                  general_frame_tx_nxt = 1'b1;
5259                               end
5260       
5261                            // invalid - wait for next frame
5262                            else
5263                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
                                   ==>
5264                          end
5265       
5266                      7'b0101010 : // versionPTP and messageType in PTP version 2
5267                         begin
5268                            // correct address and versionPTP for version 2
5269                  //          if (ptp_ver_2 & transmit_data_buf [15:8] == 8'h02)
5270                            if (ptp_ver_2 & transmit_data_buf [11:8] == 4'h2)
                                -66-  
5271                               begin
5272                                  ptp_ver_1_nxt  = 1'b0;
5273                                  // sync frame
5274                                  if (~general_frame_tx & transmit_data_buf[3:0] == 4'h0)
                                      -67-  
5275                                     begin
5276                                        tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV4_2;
                                            ==>
5277                                        sync_frame_tx_nxt = 1'b1;
5278                                        ptp_timestamp_position = tx_ptp_count;
5279                                        ptp_timestamp_position_cap   = 1'b1;
5280                                     end
5281                                  // delay_req frame
5282                                  else if (~general_frame_tx & transmit_data_buf[3:0] == 4'h1)
                                           -68-  
5283                                     begin
5284                                        tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV4_2;
                                            ==>
5285                                        delay_req_tx_nxt  = 1'b1;
5286                                     end
5287                                  // unicast pdelay req frame
5288                                  else if (ptp_unicast & ~general_frame_tx & transmit_data_buf[3:0] == 4'h2)
                                           -69-  
5289                                     begin
5290                                        tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV4_2;
                                            ==>
5291                                        pdelay_req_tx_nxt = 1'b1;
5292                                     end
5293                                  // unicast pdelay_req frame
5294                                  else if (ptp_unicast & ~general_frame_tx & transmit_data_buf[3:0] == 4'h3)
                                           -70-  
5295                                     begin
5296                                        tx_dec_state_nxt   = TX_DEC_IPV4_2;
                                            ==>
5297                                        pdelay_resp_tx_nxt = 1'b1;
5298                                     end
5299                                  // detect General 1588 Messages then wait for next frame and also if
5300                                  // invalid - wait for next frame
5301                                  else
5302                                  begin
5303                                    general_frame_tx_nxt =  ptp_pri_final_general_chk;
                                        ==>
5304                                    tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
5305                                  end
5306                                end
5307                            // correct address and versionPTP for version 1
5308                 //           else if (transmit_data_buf [15:8] == 8'h01) // ptp_ver_1 has to be 1 here ..
5309                            else if (transmit_data_buf [11:8] == 4'h1) // ptp_ver_1 has to be 1 here ..
                                     -71-  
5310                               begin
5311                                  ptp_ver_2_nxt  = 1'b0;
                                      ==>
5312                                  tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV4_2;
5313                               end
5314                            // invalid - wait for next frame
5315                            else
5316                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
                                   ==>
5317                         end
5318       
5319                      7'b1001010 : // control in PTP version 1
5320                         begin
5321                            // correct address and versionPTP for version 1
5322                            if (ptp_ver_1)
                                -72-  
5323                               begin
5324                                  // sync frame
5325                                  if (~general_frame_tx & transmit_data_buf[3:0] == 4'h0)
                                      -73-  
5326                                     begin
5327                                        tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV4_2;
                                            ==>
5328                                        sync_frame_tx_nxt = 1'b1;
5329                                        ptp_timestamp_position = tx_ptp_count;
5330                                        ptp_timestamp_position_cap_v1   = 1'b1;
5331                                     end
5332                                  // delay_req frame
5333                                  else if (~general_frame_tx & transmit_data_buf[3:0] == 4'h1)
                                           -74-  
5334                                     begin
5335                                        tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV4_2;
                                            ==>
5336                                        delay_req_tx_nxt   = 1'b1;
5337                                     end
5338                                  // detect General 1588 Messages then wait for next frame and also if
5339                                  // invalid - wait for next frame
5340                                 else
5341                                  begin
5342                                    general_frame_tx_nxt =  general_frame_tx & tx_buf_234;
                                        ==>
5343                                     tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
5344                                  end
5345                                end
5346                            // invalid - wait for next frame
5347                            else
5348                              if (sync_frame_tx_nxt) // ptp_ver_2 must be set here ...
                                  -75-  
5349                                tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV4_2;
                                    ==>
5350                              else
5351                                tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
                                    ==>
5352       
5353                         end
5354       
5355       
5356                      7'b1001100 : // timestamp start position is 34B after messageType for ptp verson 2
5357                         begin
5358                            tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV4_2;
                                ==>
5359                         end
5360       
5361                      7'b1010010 : // timestamp start position is 8B after control for ptp verson 1
5362                         begin
5363                            tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV4_2;
                                ==>
5364                         end
5365       
5366                      7'b1010101 : // timestamp end position is 9B after timestamp start
5367                         begin
5368                            // this will stop tx_ptp_count after TS finished for ptp verson 2
5369                            // but need to wait longer for ptp v1
5370                            if (ptp_ver_1 == 1'b1)
                                -76-  
5371                              tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV4_2;
                                  ==>
5372                            else
5373                             tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
                                 ==>
5374                         end
5375       
5376                      7'b1011001 : // timestamp end position is 7B after timestamp start for ptp verson 1
5377                         begin
5378                           tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
                               ==>
5379                         end
5380       
5381       
5382                      default :
5383                         begin
5384                            tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV4_2;
                                ==>
5385                         end
5386       
5387                      endcase
5388                   end
5389       
5390                TX_DEC_IPV4_3 : // decode IPv4 PTP pdelay
5391                   begin

                          -77-

5395                         begin
5396                            // PTP peer

5558                                  general_frame_tx_nxt = 1'b0;
5559                               end
5560                            else if (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == 8'h40)
                                     -95-  
5561                               begin
5562                                  tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV6_2;
                                      ==>
5563                                  general_frame_tx_nxt = 1'b1;
5564                               end
5565                            // invalid - wait for next frame
5566                            else
5567                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
                                   ==>
5568                          end
5569       
5570                      7'b0111110 : // messageType
5571                         begin
5572                            // Sync frame
5573                            if (~general_frame_tx & transmit_data_buf[3:0] == 4'h0)
                                -96-  
5574                               begin
5575                                  tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV6_2;
                                      ==>
5576                                  sync_frame_tx_nxt = 1'b1;
5577                                  ptp_timestamp_position = tx_ptp_count;
5578                                  ptp_timestamp_position_cap   = 1'b1;
5579                               end
5580                            // delay_req frame
5581                            else if (~general_frame_tx & transmit_data_buf[3:0] == 4'h1)
                                     -97-  
5582                               begin
5583                                  tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV6_2;
                                      ==>
5584                                  delay_req_tx_nxt  = 1'b1;
5585                               end
5586                            // detect General 1588 Messages then wait for next frame and also if
5587                            // invalid - wait for next frame
5588                            else
5589                            begin
5590                              general_frame_tx_nxt =  general_frame_tx_dec;
                                  ==>
5591                              tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
5592                            end
5593                         end
5594       
5595                      7'b1100000 : // timestamp start position is 34B after messageType
5596                         begin
5597                            tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV6_2;
                                ==>
5598                         end
5599       
5600                      7'b1101001 : // timestamp end position is 9B after timestamp start
5601                         begin
5602                            // this will stop tx_ptp_count after TS finished
5603                            tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
                                ==>
5604                         end
5605       
5606                       default :
5607                         begin
5608                            tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV6_2;
                                ==>
5609                         end
5610       
5611                      endcase
5612                   end
5613       
5614                TX_DEC_IPV6_3 : // decode IPv6 PTP pdelay
5615                   begin
5616                      case (tx_ptp_count)
                          -98-  
5617       
5618                      7'b0101000, 7'b0101001, 7'b0101010, 7'b0101011, 7'b0101100,
5619                      7'b0101101, 7'b0101110, 7'b0101111, 7'b0110000, 7'b0110001,
5620                      7'b0110010, 7'b0110011 : // IP multicast address part
5621                         begin
5622                            // PTP primary
5623                            if (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == 8'h00)
                                -99-  
5624                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV6_3;
                                   ==>
5625                            // invalid - wait for next frame
5626                            else
5627                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
                                   ==>
5628                         end
5629       
5630                      7'b0110100 : // IP multicast address
5631                         begin
5632                            // PTP pdelay
5633                            if (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == 8'h00)
                                -100-  
5634                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV6_3;
                                   ==>
5635                            // PTP primary
5636                            else if (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == 8'h01)
                                     -101-  
5637                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV6_2;
                                   ==>
5638                            else
5639                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
                                   ==>
5640                         end
5641       
5642                      7'b0110101 : // IP multicast address
5643                         begin
5644                            // PTP primary
5645                            if (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == 8'h6b)
                                -102-  
5646                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV6_3;
                                   ==>
5647                            else
5648                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
                                   ==>
5649                         end
5650       
5651                      7'b0111000 : // UDP destination port 1
5652                         begin
5653                            if (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == 8'h01)
                                -103-  
5654                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV6_3;
                                   ==>
5655                            // invalid - wait for next frame
5656                            else
5657                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
                                   ==>
5658                          end
5659       
5660                      7'b0111001 : // UDP destination port 2
5661                         begin
5662                            if (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == 8'h3f)
                                -104-  
5663                               begin
5664                                  tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV6_3;
                                      ==>
5665                                  general_frame_tx_nxt = 1'b0;
5666                               end
5667                            else if (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == 8'h40)
                                     -105-  
5668                               begin
5669                                  tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV6_3;
                                      ==>
5670                                  general_frame_tx_nxt = 1'b1;
5671                               end
5672                            // invalid - wait for next frame
5673                            else
5674                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
                                   ==>
5675                          end
5676       
5677                      7'b0111110 : // messageType
5678                         begin
5679                            // pdelay_req frame
5680                            if (~general_frame_tx & transmit_data_buf[3:0] == 4'h2)
                                -106-  
5681                               begin
5682                                  tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV6_3;
                                      ==>
5683                                  pdelay_req_tx_nxt = 1'b1;
5684                               end
5685                            // pdelay_resp frame
5686                            else if (~general_frame_tx & transmit_data_buf[3:0] == 4'h3)
                                     -107-  
5687                               begin
5688                                  tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV6_3;
                                      ==>
5689                                  pdelay_resp_tx_nxt   = 1'b1;
5690                               end
5691                            // detect General 1588 Messages then wait for next frame and also if
5692                            // invalid - wait for next frame
5693                            else
5694                            begin
5695                              general_frame_tx_nxt =  ptp_peer_final_general_chk; // Pdelay_Resp_Follow_Up
                                  ==>
5696                              tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
5697                            end
5698                         end
5699       
5700                      default :
5701                         begin
5702                            tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IPV6_3;
                                ==>
5703                         end
5704       
5705                      endcase
5706                   end
5707       
5708                TX_DEC_VIPV4_1 : // decode IPv4
5709                   begin
5710                      case (tx_ptp_count)
                          -108-  
5711                      7'b0010001 : // Ethertype IPv4
5712                         begin
5713                            if (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == 8'h00)
                                -109-  
5714                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_VIPV4_1;
                                   ==>
5715                            // invalid - wait for next frame
5716                            else
5717                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
                                   ==>
5718                          end
5719       
5720                      7'b0011011 : // UDP protocol
5721                         begin
5722                            if (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == 8'h11)
                                -110-  
5723                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_VIPV4_1;
                                   ==>
5724                            // invalid - wait for next frame
5725                            else
5726                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
                                   ==>
5727                          end
5728       
5729                      7'b0100010 : // IP multicast address 1
5730                         begin
5731                            // PTP primary and peer
5732                            if (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == 8'he0)
                                -111-  
5733                               begin
5734                                  tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_VIPV4_1;
5735                                  if (ptp_unicast_ena_sync &
                                      -112-  
5736                                      (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == tx_ptp_unicast[31:24]))
5737                                     ptp_unicast_nxt   = 1'b1;
                                         ==>
                                         MISSING_ELSE
                                         ==>
5738                               end
5739                            // PTP unicast
5740                            else if (ptp_unicast_ena_sync &
                                     -113-  
5741                                     (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == tx_ptp_unicast[31:24]))
5742                               begin
5743                                  tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_VIPV4_1;
                                      ==>
5744                                  ptp_unicast_nxt   = 1'b1;
5745                               end
5746                            // invalid - wait for next frame
5747                            else
5748                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
                                   ==>
5749                         end
5750       
5751                      7'b0100011 : // IP multicast address 2
5752                         begin
5753                            // PTP primary and peer, not unicast
5754                            if (~ptp_unicast & (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == 8'h00))
                                -114-  
5755                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_VIPV4_1;
                                   ==>
5756                            // PTP unicast
5757                            else if (ptp_unicast &
                                     -115-  
5758                                     (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == tx_ptp_unicast[23:16]))
5759                               begin
5760                                  tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_VIPV4_1;
                                      ==>
5761                                  ptp_unicast_nxt   = 1'b1;
5762                               end
5763                            // invalid - wait for next frame
5764                            else
5765                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
                                   ==>
5766                         end
5767       
5768                      7'b0100100 : // IP multicast address 3
5769                         begin
5770                            // PTP primary, not unicast
5771                            if (~ptp_unicast & (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == 8'h01))
                                -116-  
5772                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_VIPV4_2;
                                   ==>
5773                            // peer delay, not unicast
5774                            else if (~ptp_unicast & (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == 8'h00))
                                     -117-  
5775                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_VIPV4_3;
                                   ==>
5776                            // PTP unicast
5777                            else if (ptp_unicast &
                                     -118-  
5778                                     (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == tx_ptp_unicast[15:8]))
5779                               begin
5780                                  tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_VIPV4_2;
                                      ==>
5781                                  ptp_unicast_nxt   = 1'b1;
5782                               end
5783                            // invalid - wait for next frame
5784                            else
5785                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
                                   ==>
5786                         end
5787       
5788                      default :
5789                         begin
5790                            tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_VIPV4_1;
                                ==>
5791                         end
5792       
5793                      endcase
5794                   end
5795       
5796                TX_DEC_VIPV4_2 : // decode IPv4 PTP primary version 1 and 2
5797                   begin
5798                      case (tx_ptp_count)
                          -119-  
5799       
5800                      7'b0100101 : // IP multicast address 4
5801                         begin
5802                            // PTP primary version 1 and 2 possible, not unicast
5803                            if (~ptp_unicast & (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == 8'h81))
                                -120-  
5804                               begin
5805                                  tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_VIPV4_2;
                                      ==>
5806                                  ptp_ver_1_nxt     = 1'b1;
5807                                  ptp_ver_2_nxt     = 1'b1;
5808                               end
5809                            // PTP primary version 1, not unicast
5810                            else if (ptp_primary_nunicast)
                                     -121-  
5811                               begin
5812                                  tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_VIPV4_2;
                                      ==>
5813                                  ptp_ver_1_nxt     = 1'b1;
5814                               end
5815                            // PTP unicast
5816                            else if (ptp_unicast &
                                     -122-  
5817                                     (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == tx_ptp_unicast[7:0]))
5818                               begin
5819                                  tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_VIPV4_2;
                                      ==>
5820                                  ptp_unicast_nxt   = 1'b1;
5821                                  ptp_ver_2_nxt     = 1'b1;
5822                               end
5823                            // invalid - wait for next frame
5824                            else
5825                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
                                   ==>
5826                         end
5827       
5828                      7'b0101000 : // UDP destination port 1
5829                         begin
5830                            if (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == 8'h01)
                                -123-  
5831                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_VIPV4_2;
                                   ==>
5832                            // invalid - wait for next frame
5833                            else
5834                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
                                   ==>
5835                          end
5836       
5837                      7'b0101001 : // UDP destination port 2
5838                         begin
5839                            if (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == 8'h3f)
                                -124-  
5840                               begin
5841                                  tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_VIPV4_2;
                                      ==>
5842                                  general_frame_tx_nxt = 1'b0;
5843                               end
5844                            else if (transmit_data_buf[7:0] == 8'h40)
                                     -125-  
5845                               begin
5846                                  tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_VIPV4_2;
                                      ==>
5847                                  general_frame_tx_nxt = 1'b1;
5848                               end
5849                            // invalid - wait for next frame
5850                            else
5851                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
                                   ==>
5852                          end
5853       
5854                      7'b0101110 : // versionPTP and messageType in PTP version 2
5855                         begin
5856                            // correct address and versionPTP for version 2
5857                  //          if (ptp_ver_2 & transmit_data_buf [15:8] == 8'h02)
5858                            if (ptp_ver_2 & transmit_data_buf [11:8] == 4'h2)
                                -126-  
5859                               begin
5860                                  ptp_ver_1_nxt  = 1'b0;
5861                                  // sync frame
5862                                  if (~general_frame_tx & transmit_data_buf[3:0] == 4'h0)
                                      -127-  
5863                                     begin
5864                                        tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_VIPV4_2;
                                            ==>
5865                                        sync_frame_tx_nxt = 1'b1;
5866                                        ptp_timestamp_position = tx_ptp_count;
5867                                        ptp_timestamp_position_cap   = 1'b1;
5868                                     end
5869                                  // delay_req frame
5870                                  else if (~general_frame_tx & transmit_data_buf[3:0] == 4'h1)
                                           -128-  
5871                                     begin
5872                                        tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_VIPV4_2;
                                            ==>
5873                                        delay_req_tx_nxt  = 1'b1;
5874                                     end
5875                                  // unicast pdelay req frame
5876                                  else if (~general_frame_tx & ptp_unicast & transmit_data_buf[3:0] == 4'h2)
                                           -129-  
5877                                     begin
5878                                        tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_VIPV4_2;
                                            ==>
5879                                        pdelay_req_tx_nxt = 1'b1;
5880                                     end
5881                                  // unicast pdelay_req frame
5882                                  else if (~general_frame_tx & ptp_unicast & transmit_data_buf[3:0] == 4'h3)
                                           -130-  
5883                                     begin
5884                                        tx_dec_state_nxt   = TX_DEC_VIPV4_2;
                                            ==>
5885                                        pdelay_resp_tx_nxt = 1'b1;
5886                                     end
5887                                  // detect General 1588 Messages then wait for next frame and also if
5888                                  // invalid - wait for next frame
5889                                  else
5890                                  begin
5891                                    general_frame_tx_nxt = ptp_pri_final_general_chk;
                                        ==>
5892                                    tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
5893                                  end
5894                                end
5895                            // correct address and versionPTP for version 1
5896                    //        else if (transmit_data_buf [15:8] == 8'h01) // ptp_ver_1 must be set in here ...
5897                            else if (transmit_data_buf [11:8] == 4'h1) // ptp_ver_1 must be set in here ...
                                     -131-  
5898                               begin
5899                                  ptp_ver_2_nxt  = 1'b0;
                                      ==>
5900                                  tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_VIPV4_2;
5901                               end
5902                            // invalid - wait for next frame
5903                            else
5904                               tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
                                   ==>
5905                         end
5906       
5907                      7'b1001110 : // control in PTP version 1
5908                         begin
5909                            // correct address and versionPTP for version 1
5910                            if (ptp_ver_1)
                                -132-  
5911                               begin
5912                                  // sync frame
5913                                  if (~general_frame_tx & transmit_data_buf[3:0] == 4'h0)
                                      -133-  
5914                                     begin
5915                                        tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_VIPV4_2;
                                            ==>
5916                                        sync_frame_tx_nxt = 1'b1;
5917                                        ptp_timestamp_position = tx_ptp_count;
5918                                        ptp_timestamp_position_cap_v1   = 1'b1;
5919                                     end
5920                                  // delay_req frame
5921                                  else if (~general_frame_tx & transmit_data_buf[3:0] == 4'h1)
                                           -134-

5923                                        tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_VIPV4_2;
                                            ==>
5924                                        delay_req_tx_nxt   = 1'b1;
5925                                     end
5926                                  // detect General 1588 Messages then wait for next frame and also if
5927                                  // invalid - wait for next frame
5928                                  else
5929                                  begin
5930                                    general_frame_tx_nxt =  general_frame_tx & tx_buf_234;
                                        ==>
5931                                    tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
5932                                  end
5933                                end
5934                            // invalid - wait for next frame
5935                            else
5936                              if (sync_frame_tx_nxt) // ptp_ver_2 must be set here ..
                                  -135-

                                    ==>
5938                              else
5939                                tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
                                    ==>
5940                         end
5941       
5942                      7'b1010000 : // timestamp start position is 34B after messageType
5943                         begin
5944                            tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_VIPV4_2;
                                ==>
5945                         end
5946       
5947                      7'b1010110 : // // timestamp start position is 8B after control for ptp verson 1
5948                         begin
5949                            tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_VIPV4_2;
                                ==>
5950                         end
5951       
5952                      7'b1011001 : // timestamp end position is 9B after timestamp start
5953                         begin
5954                            // this will stop tx_ptp_count after TS finished for ptp verson 2
5955                            // but need to wait longer for ptp v1
5956                            if (ptp_ver_1 == 1'b1)
                                -136-  
5957                              tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_VIPV4_2;
                                  ==>
5958                            else
5959                             tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
                                 ==>
5960                         end
5961       
5962                      7'b1011101 : // timestamp end position is 7B after timestamp start for ptp verson 1
5963                         begin
5964                           tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_IDLE;
                               ==>
5965                         end
5966       
5967                      default :
5968                         begin
5969                            tx_dec_state_nxt  = TX_DEC_VIPV4_2;
                                ==>
5970                         end
5971       
5972                      endcase
5973                   end

                          -137-

6046                TX_DEC_VIPV6_1 : // decode IPv6

                          -144-
